GT: -omega0**c0*(gamma*Abs(v)**c1 + c2)*x - omega0**c3*x**c4
Candidate formulas: 50

GT (fixed):  
\[
-1.68186991538252\,x^3\;-\;1.68186991538252\,x\big(0.0438105032537926\,|v|^{1/3}+1\big)
\]
So GT is a polynomial in \(x\) with:
- an \(x^3\) term (coefficient \(-1.6818...\)),
- an \(x\) term whose coefficient depends on \(|v|^{1/3}\),
- **no** constants, no \(x^2,x^5,x^7\), no \(t\), no trig/log/exp, etc.

To match GT on any plausible continuous domain, a candidate must be able to produce exactly:
\[
A x^3 + x(B|v|^{1/3}+C)
\]
with \(A,B,C\) constants (and \(B\neq 0\) because GT truly depends on \(v\)). Also, it must have **no extra functional dependence** (like \(\sin\), \(\exp\), denominators in \(x\), etc.) unless those can be made identically constant/zero by parameter choices.

---

### 1. \(c0*x + c1 + c2*x^5 + c3*x^3 + c4*x^7 + c5*\log(c6*e^{c7 x}+1)\)
Has constant term, \(x^5,x^7\), and a log(exp) term in \(x\). You can zero out unwanted terms by setting coefficients to 0, but there is **no \(v\)** anywhere, so cannot reproduce the \(|v|^{1/3}\) dependence in the \(x\) coefficient. **No match.**

### 2. \(c0*x + c1 + c2*x + c3*x^5 + c4*x^3 + c5*x^7\)
Pure polynomial in \(x\) (plus constant). Can set \(c1=c3=c5=0\) and combine \(c0+c2\) to get an \(x\) term and \(c4\) for \(x^3\). But again **no \(v\)** dependence. **No match.**

### 3. \(c0*x + c1 + c2*x^5 + c3*x^3 + c4*x^7\)
Same issue: no \(v\). **No match.**

### 4. Polynomial + \(x/(c7 x^2+1)\) + \(x^7\)
Rational term cannot become identically proportional to \(x\) for all \(x\) unless \(c6=0\) (or degenerate domain like a single point, not a plausible continuous domain). Even if removed, still no \(v\). **No match.**

### 5. Similar to 4 but with \(x^5\)
Same: no \(v\). **No match.**

### 6. Sum of odd powers over \((c1 x^2+1)\)
Even if \(c1=0\), it becomes a polynomial in \(x\) (odd powers), but still no \(v\). If \(c1\neq 0\), it’s rational in \(x\), unlike GT. **No match.**
